msg:The hotel is located at Capital Airport T3, about 5 minutes by car. It is 7.2 kilometers away from the National Exhibition Center, about 15 minutes by car, and 17 kilometers to the Chaoyang Pavilion. The hotel is a high-end star hotel within the airport area.
